0006f1c2     #define SDF_BASE_MIN 0.125
0006f1e1     #define SDF_BASE_MAX 0.25
0006f1ff     #define SDF_BASE_DEV -0.65
0006f21e #endif

0006f434 precision mediump float;
0006f44e #ifndef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
0006f471     #define highp mediump
0006f48b #endif
0006f493 uniform float cbuffer0_ps[8];
0006f4b1 uniform float cbuffer1_ps[128];
0006f4d2 uniform sampler2D pattern;
0006f4ed uniform sampler2D ramps;
0006f506 uniform sampler2D image;
0006f51f uniform sampler2D glyphs;
0006f539 uniform sampler2D shadow;
0006f554 out lowp vec4 fragColor;

0006f76a lowp vec4 main_brush(highp vec2 uv);
0006f78f lowp vec4 main_effect();
0006f7a9 ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
0006f80e void main()
0006f81c     /////////////////////////////////////////////////////
0006f856     // Fetch paint color and opacity
0006f87b     /////////////////////////////////////////////////////
0006f8b5     #if defined(PAINT_SOLID)
0006f8d2         lowp vec4 paint = color;
0006f8f3         lowp float opacity_ = 1.0;
0006f916     #endif
0006f922     #if defined(PAINT_LINEAR)
0006f940         lowp vec4 paint = texture(ramps, uv0);
0006f96f         lowp float opacity_ = cbuffer0_ps[0];
0006f99d     #endif
0006f9a9     #if defined(PAINT_RADIAL)
0006f9c7         float dd = cbuffer0_ps[4] * uv0.x - cbuffer0_ps[5] * uv0.y;
0006fa0b         float u = cbuffer0_ps[0] * uv0.x + cbuffer0_ps[1] * uv0.y + cbuffer0_ps[2] * 
0006fa61             sqrt(uv0.x * uv0.x + uv0.y * uv0.y - dd * dd);
0006fa9c         lowp vec4 paint = texture(ramps, vec2(u, cbuffer0_ps[6]));
0006fadf         lowp float opacity_ = cbuffer0_ps[3];
0006fb0d     #endif
0006fb19     #if defined(PAINT_PATTERN)
0006fb38         #if defined(CUSTOM_PATTERN)
0006fb5c             lowp vec4 paint = main_brush(uv0);
0006fb8b         #endif
0006fb9a         #if defined(CLAMP_PATTERN)
0006fbbd             lowp float inside = float(uv0 == clamp(uv0, rect.xy, rect.zw));
0006fc09             lowp vec4 paint = inside * texture(pattern, uv0);
0006fc47         #endif
0006fc56         #if defined(REPEAT_PATTERN) || defined(MIRRORU_PATTERN) || defined(MIRRORV_PATTERN) || defined(MIRROR_PATTERN)
0006fccd             highp vec2 uv = (uv0 - tile.xy) / tile.zw;
0006fd04             #if defined(REPEAT_PATTERN)
0006fd2c                 uv = fract(uv);
0006fd4c             #endif
0006fd5f             #if defined(MIRRORU_PATTERN)
0006fd88                 uv.x = abs(uv.x - 2.0 * floor((uv.x - 1.0) / 2.0) - 2.0);
0006fdd2                 uv.y = fract(uv.y);
0006fdf6             #endif
0006fe09             #if defined(MIRRORV_PATTERN)
0006fe32                 uv.x = fract(uv.x);
0006fe56                 uv.y = abs(uv.y - 2.0 * floor((uv.y - 1.0) / 2.0) - 2.0);
0006fea0             #endif
0006feb3             #if defined(MIRROR_PATTERN)
0006fedb                 uv = abs(uv - 2.0 * floor((uv - 1.0) / 2.0) - 2.0);
0006ff1f             #endif
0006ff32             uv = uv * tile.zw + tile.xy;
0006ff5b             lowp float inside = float(uv == clamp(uv, rect.xy, rect.zw));
0006ffa5             lowp vec4 paint = inside * textureGrad(pattern, uv, dFdx(uv0), dFdy(uv0));
0006fffc         #endif
0007000b         #if !defined(CUSTOM_PATTERN) && !defined(CLAMP_PATTERN) && !defined(REPEAT_PATTERN) && !defined(MIRRORU_PATTERN) && !defined(MIRRORV_PATTERN) && !defined(MIRROR_PATTERN)
000700bd             lowp vec4 paint = texture(pattern, uv0);
000700f2         #endif
00070101         lowp float opacity_ = cbuffer0_ps[0];
0007012f     #endif
0007013b     /////////////////////////////////////////////////////
00070175     // Apply selected effect
00070192     /////////////////////////////////////////////////////
000701cc     #if defined(EFFECT_RGBA)
000701e9         fragColor = vec4(cbuffer0_ps[0], cbuffer0_ps[1], cbuffer0_ps[2], cbuffer0_ps[3]);
00070243     #endif
0007024f     #if defined(EFFECT_MASK)
0007026c         fragColor = vec4(1);
00070289     #endif
00070295     #if defined(EFFECT_CLEAR)
000702b3         fragColor = vec4(0);
000702d0     #endif
000702dc     #if defined(EFFECT_PATH)
000702f9         fragColor = opacity_ * paint;
0007031f     #endif
0007032b     #if defined(EFFECT_PATH_AA)
0007034b         fragColor = (opacity_ * coverage) * paint;
0007037e     #endif
0007038a     #if defined(EFFECT_OPACITY)
000703aa         fragColor = texture(image, uv1) * (opacity_ * paint.a);
000703ea     #endif
000703f6     #if defined(EFFECT_SHADOW)
00070415         lowp vec4 shadowColor = vec4(cbuffer1_ps[0], cbuffer1_ps[1], cbuffer1_ps[2], cbuffer1_ps[3]);
0007047b         vec2 offset = vec2(cbuffer1_ps[4], -cbuffer1_ps[5]);
000704b8         vec2 uv = clamp(uv1 - offset, rect.xy, rect.zw);
000704f1         lowp float alpha = mix(texture(image, uv).a, texture(shadow, uv).a, cbuffer1_ps[6]);
0007054e         lowp vec4 img = texture(image, clamp(uv1, rect.xy, rect.zw));
00070594         fragColor = (img + (1.0 - img.a) * (shadowColor * alpha)) * (opacity_ * paint.a);
000705ee     #endif
000705fa     #if defined(EFFECT_BLUR)
00070617         fragColor = mix(texture(image, uv1), texture(shadow, uv1), cbuffer1_ps[0]) * (opacity_ * paint.a);
00070682     #endif
0007068e     #if defined(EFFECT_SDF)
000706aa         float distance = SDF_SCALE * (texture(glyphs, uv1).r - SDF_BIAS);
000706f4         float gradLen = length(dFdx(st1));
0007071f         float scale = 1.0 / gradLen;

00071492         float dd = cbuffer0_ps[4] * uv0.x - cbuffer0_ps[5] * uv0.y;
000714d6         float u = cbuffer0_ps[0] * uv0.x + cbuffer0_ps[1] * uv0.y + cbuffer0_ps[2] * 
0007152c             sqrt(uv0.x * uv0.x + uv0.y * uv0.y - dd * dd);

00071716         #endif

000717fb                 uv = fract(uv);
0007181b             #endif

000718a1                 uv.y = fract(uv.y);
000718c5             #endif

00071ad0         #endif
